				GER = { has_capitulated = yes }
				GER = { is_subject = yes }
			}

			has_army_manpower = { size > 1000000 }
			
			OR = { #borders swi
				any_neighbor_country = { tag = SWI }
				any_allied_country = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT any_neighbor_country = { tag = SWI } }
			}
			
			#swi is a threat
			SWI = { EAI_is_threat = yes }

			NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }

			OR = { #pol is no threat
				POL = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			
			OR = { #fra is no threat
				FRA = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }

				add_ideas = syndicalism_influence
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { GER = {  has_government = socialism } }
				add_ideas = socialism_influence
			}
				country_event = { id = generic.1 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = neutrality_idea }
					remove_ideas = neutrality_idea
				}
			}
		}
	}

focus = {
	id = GER_soviet_invasion
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_major_war
	prerequisite = { focus = GER_poland_friend focus = GER_war_with_poland focus = GER_danzig_or_war}
	bypass = {
			OR = {
				SOV = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				NOT = { country_exists = SOV }
				GER = { has_war_with = SOV}
			}
		}
	available = {
		country_exists = SOV
	}
	x = 35
	y = 6
	cost = 10
	historical_ai = { #EAI
			has_fascist_government = yes
		
			date > 1941.4.1
			
			NOT = { #has not lost
				GER = { has_capitulated = yes }
				GER = { is_subject = yes }
			}
		
			#army requirement
			has_army_manpower = { size > 2500000 }
			OR = {
				has_army_size = { type = armor size > 20 }
				has_army_manpower = { type = armor size > 200000 }
				date > 1941.8.1
			}
			
			OR = { #borders sov
				any_neighbor_country = { tag = SOV }
				any_allied_country = { is_neighbor_of = ROOT any_neighbor_country = { tag = SOV } }
			}
			
			#sov is a threat
			SOV = { EAI_is_threat = yes }
			
			#no current enemies to deal with
			NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
		
			OR = { #pol is no threat
				POL = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			
			OR = { #fra is no threat
				FRA = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			
			OR = { #den is no threat
				DEN = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
			
			OR = { #yug is no threat
				YUG = { NOT = { EAI_is_threat = yes } }
				NOT = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
			}
		}
	ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { #EAI
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #AI should not pick this focus if it does not share a border with the Soviets
				NOT = { 
					any_home_area_neighbor_country = {
						tag = SOV
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				date < 1939.1.1
			}
		}
	completion_reward = {
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = SOV
			generator = { 219 }
		}
	}	
}
